E.g. s-anand.net\n• Server: The IP address of the server.\nThe fields are separated by spaces and quoted by double quotes ("). Unlike CSV files, quoted fields are escaped via \\" and not "". If 200 <= Status < 300 it is a successful request\n• Size: The size of the response in bytes. E.g. 1234\n• Referer: The referer URL. E.g. https://s-anand.net/\n• User agent: The browser used. This will contain spaces and might have escaped quotes.\n• Vhost: The virtual host. E.g. s-anand.net\n• Server: The IP address of the server.\n\nThe fields are separated by spaces and quoted by double quotes ("). Unlike CSV files, quoted fields are escaped via \\" and not "".
